<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стность</a> (8279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvéstnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvéstnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известность.html>изве́стности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<ol><li>reputation, fame, repute, notoriety, renown</li>
<li>publicity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> celebrity, prominent figure, notability</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvéstnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изве́стнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)изве́стней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известнейший.html>изве́стнейший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>known, familiar</li>
<li>well-known, renowned, famous</li>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a> (12260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄσβεστος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ásbestos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ízvestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>и́звести</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>и́звести</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звестей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lime <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">calcium oxide, quicklime</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гашёная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gašónaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slaked lime, slack lime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">негашёная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">negašónaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">quicklime, burnt lime</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">хло́рная <a href = vnd.unilang:известь.html>и́звесть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xlórnaja ízvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">chloride of lime, bleaching powder</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извещать.html>извеща́ть</a> (15682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извещать.html>извеща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izveščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́ть</a></b>)

***извиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a> (9186)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:виться.html>ви́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изви́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to coil, to wriggle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извиваться.html>извива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvivátʹsja</b> ot bóli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to writhe with pain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(river, road etc)</i> to twist, to wind, to meander</li></ol>

***извинить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́ть</a> (1293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:винить.html>вини́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинять.html>извиня́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a> (7912)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">извле́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izvlék-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvlekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извлечь.html>извле́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to extract, to elicit, to draw out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> чего́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> štó-libo iz čevó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive something from something</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:урок.html>уро́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> urók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to learn a lesson (from); to moralize, to draw the moral</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:польза.html>по́льзу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> pólʹzu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive benefit (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прибыть.html>при́были</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> ogrómnyje príbyli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive / make huge profits (from)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:извлекать.html>извлека́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvlekátʹ</b> udovólʹstvije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to derive pleasure (from)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***изводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a> (16406)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:известить.html>извести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to use up, to spend</li>
<li>to exterminate</li>
<li>to exhaust
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvodítʹ</b> sebjá rabótoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overwork oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to torment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:изводить.html>изводи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:насмешка.html>насме́шками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>izvodítʹ</b> nasméškami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bait</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to vex, to exasperate</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
